     1→"""Reality signal computation from search results."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→
     6→def compute_signal(
     7→    repos: list[dict],
     8→    hn_posts: list[dict],
     9→    top_similarity: float | None = None,
    10→) -> dict:
    11→    """Compute a 0-100 reality signal from search results.
    12→
    13→    Args:
    14→        repos: GitHub repository results.
    15→        hn_posts: Hacker News post results.
    16→        top_similarity: Optional average cosine similarity of the top results
    17→            to the query embedding (0–1). When provided, a semantic boost
    18→            component is added to the breakdown and score.
    19→
    20→    Returns:
    21→        Dict with ``score``, ``verdict``, and ``breakdown``.
    22→    """
    23→    # GitHub component (0-60)
    24→    total_repos = len(repos)
    25→    max_stars = max((r["stars"] for r in repos), default=0)
    26→
    27→    if total_repos == 0:
    28→        gh_score = 0
    29→    elif total_repos <= 3:
    30→        gh_score = 15
    31→    elif total_repos <= 7:
    32→        gh_score = 30
    33→    else:
    34→        gh_score = 45
    35→
    36→    if max_stars >= 5000:
    37→        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 20)
    38→    elif max_stars >= 1000:
    39→        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 15)
    40→    elif max_stars >= 100:
    41→        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 10)
    42→
    43→    # HN component (0-40)
    44→    total_hn = len(hn_posts)
    45→    max_points = max((p["points"] for p in hn_posts), default=0)
    46→
    47→    if total_hn == 0:
    48→        hn_score = 0
    49→    elif total_hn <= 2:
    50→        hn_score = 10
    51→    else:
    52→        hn_score = 25
    53→
    54→    if max_points >= 100:
    55→        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 15)
    56→    elif max_points >= 30:
    57→        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 10)
    58→
    59→    # Semantic component (0-20): rewards conceptually similar results
    60→    semantic_score = 0
    61→    if top_similarity is not None:
    62→        if top_similarity >= 0.8:
    63→            semantic_score = 20
    64→        elif top_similarity >= 0.6:
    65→            semantic_score = 15
    66→        elif top_similarity >= 0.4:
    67→            semantic_score = 10
    68→        elif top_similarity >= 0.2:
    69→            semantic_score = 5
    70→
    71→    score = min(100, gh_score + hn_score + semantic_score)
    72→
    73→    if score < 30:
    74→        verdict = "LOW"
    75→    elif score <= 60:
    76→        verdict = "MODERATE"
    77→    else:
    78→        verdict = "HIGH"
    79→
    80→    breakdown: dict[str, int] = {"github": gh_score, "hn": hn_score}
    81→    if top_similarity is not None:
    82→        breakdown["semantic"] = semantic_score
    83→
    84→    return {
    85→        "score": score,
    86→        "verdict": verdict,
    87→        "breakdown": breakdown,
    88→    }
    89→

    10→from priorart import __version__
    11→from priorart.scoring import compute_signal
    12→from priorart.sources.github import search_repos
    13→from priorart.sources.hn import search_discussions
    14→
    15→
    16→def _result_text(item: dict, kind: str) -> str:
    17→    """Extract a single text string to embed from a result item."""
    18→    if kind == "repo":
    19→        name = item.get("name") or ""
    20→        desc = item.get("description") or ""
    21→        return f"{name} {desc}".strip()
    22→    # hn
    23→    return item.get("title") or ""
    24→
    25→
    26→def build_queries(title: str, body: str = "") -> list[str]:
    27→    """Build search queries from the idea title (and optional body).
    28→
    29→    Uses the title directly plus cleaned variants.
    30→    The title IS the idea description — no LLM needed.
    31→    """
    32→    clean = title.strip()
    33→    for prefix in ["idea:", "idea -", "[idea]"]:
    34→        if clean.lower().startswith(prefix):
    35→            clean = clean[len(prefix) :].strip()
    36→
    37→    queries: list[str] = []
    38→    seen: set[str] = set()
    39→
    40→    def add(q: str) -> None:
    41→        q = q.strip()
    42→        if q and q.lower() not in seen:
    43→            seen.add(q.lower())
    44→            queries.append(q)
    45→
    46→    # Split on common separators
    47→    parts = [clean]
    48→    for sep in [" — ", " - ", " – ", " | "]:
    49→        if sep in clean:
    50→            parts = [p.strip() for p in clean.split(sep) if p.strip()]
    51→            break
    52→
    53→    for part in parts:
    54→        stripped = re.sub(r"\([^)]*\)", "", part).strip()
    55→        stripped = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", stripped).strip()
    56→        stripped = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", stripped)
    57→        if stripped:
    58→            if len(stripped.split()) <= 1 and len(parts) > 1:
    59→                continue
    60→            add(stripped)
    61→
    62→    full = " ".join(queries)
    63→    words = full.split()
    64→    if len(words) > 5:
    65→        add(" ".join(words[:5]))
    66→        add(" ".join(words[:3]))
    67→
    68→    if body:
    69→        for line in body.split("
"):
    70→            line = line.strip().strip("#").strip("-").strip("*").strip()
    71→            if len(line) > 10 and not line.startswith(("http", "![", "<!--")):
    72→                body_clean = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", line).strip()
    73→                body_clean = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", body_clean)
    74→                body_words = body_clean.split()
    75→                if len(body_words) >= 3:
    76→                    add(" ".join(body_words[:6]))
    77→                    break
    78→
    79→    return queries
    80→
    81→
    82→def scan(
    83→    idea: str,
    84→    github_token: str | None = None,
    85→    sources: list[str] | None = None,
    86→    body: str = "",
    87→    openai_key: str | None = None,
    88→) -> dict:
    89→    """Run a full prior-art scan and return structured results.
    90→
    91→    Args:
    92→        idea: The idea description to scan.
    93→        github_token: GitHub personal access token (required for GitHub source).
    94→        sources: List of source names to query. Defaults to ["github", "hn"].
    95→        body: Optional body text for additional query extraction.
    96→        openai_key: OpenAI API key. When provided, results are reranked by
    97→            cosine similarity to the idea embedding and the signal score
    98→            incorporates a semantic component.
    99→
   100→    Returns:
   101→        Structured dict: {query, queries, sources, signal, meta}
   102→    """
   103→    if sources is None:
   104→        sources = ["github", "hn"]
   105→
   106→    queries = build_queries(idea, body)
   107→
   108→    all_repos: list[dict] = []
   109→    all_hn: list[dict] = []
   110→    seen_repo_names: set[str] = set()
   111→    seen_hn_urls: set[str] = set()
   112→
   113→    for query in queries:
   114→        if "github" in sources:
   115→            repos = search_repos(query, github_token)
   116→            for r in repos:
   117→                if r["name"] not in seen_repo_names:
   118→                    seen_repo_names.add(r["name"])
   119→                    all_repos.append(r)
   120→            time.sleep(1)
   121→
   122→        if "hn" in sources:
   123→            hn = search_discussions(query)
   124→            for h in hn:
   125→                if h["url"] not in seen_hn_urls:
   126→                    seen_hn_urls.add(h["url"])
   127→                    all_hn.append(h)
   128→            time.sleep(0.5)
   129→
   130→    all_repos.sort(key=lambda r: r["stars"], reverse=True)
   131→    all_hn.sort(key=lambda h: h["points"], reverse=True)
   132→
   133→    # Semantic reranking — only when an OpenAI key is supplied and there are results
   134→    top_similarity: float | None = None
   135→    if openai_key and (all_repos or all_hn):
   136→        try:
   137→            from priorart.embeddings import embed_texts, rank_by_similarity
   138→
   139→            repo_texts = [_result_text(r, "repo") for r in all_repos]
   140→            hn_texts = [_result_text(h, "hn") for h in all_hn]
   141→            all_texts = [idea] + repo_texts + hn_texts
   142→
   143→            embeddings = embed_texts(all_texts, openai_key)
   144→            query_vec = embeddings[0]
   145→            repo_embeddings = embeddings[1 : len(all_repos) + 1]
   146→            hn_embeddings = embeddings[len(all_repos) + 1 :]
   147→
   148→            if all_repos:
   149→                all_repos = rank_by_similarity(query_vec, all_repos, repo_embeddings)
   150→            if all_hn:
   151→                all_hn = rank_by_similarity(query_vec, all_hn, hn_embeddings)
   152→
   153→            # Average similarity of top-3 across both sources
   154→            top_sims = (
   155→                [r["similarity"] for r in all_repos[:3]]
   156→                + [h["similarity"] for h in all_hn[:3]]
   157→            )
   158→            if top_sims:
   159→                top_similarity = sum(top_sims) / len(top_sims)
   160→        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   161→            print(f"Warning: semantic reranking failed ({exc})", file=sys.stderr)
   162→
   163→    signal = compute_signal(all_repos, all_hn, top_similarity)
   164→
   165→    source_results = []
   166→    if "github" in sources:
   167→        source_results.append({"type": "github", "results": all_repos})
   168→    if "hn" in sources:
   169→        source_results.append({"type": "hn", "results": all_hn})
   170→
   171→    return {
   172→        "query": idea,
   173→        "queries": queries,
   174→        "sources": source_results,
   175→        "signal": signal,
   176→        "meta": {
   177→            "timestamp": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
   178→            "version": __version__,
   179→        },
   180→    }

     1→"""GitHub repository search source."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import sys
     6→
     7→import httpx
     8→
     9→GITHUB_API = "https://api.github.com"
    10→
    11→
    12→def search_repos(
    13→    query: str,
    14→    token: str | None = None,
    15→    max_results: int = 10,
    16→) -> list[dict]:
    17→    """Search GitHub for repositories matching the query."""
    18→    headers = {
    19→        "Accept": "application/vnd.github+json",
    20→        "X-GitHub-Api-Version": "2022-11-28",
    21→    }
    22→    if token:
    23→        headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {token}"
    24→    url = f"{GITHUB_API}/search/repositories"
    25→    params = {
    26→        "q": query,
    27→        "sort": "stars",
    28→        "order": "desc",
    29→        "per_page": max_results,
    30→    }
    31→    try:
    32→        resp = httpx.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=15)
    33→        resp.raise_for_status()
    34→        data = resp.json()
    35→        return [
    36→            {
    37→                "name": r["full_name"],
    38→                "stars": r["stargazers_count"],
    39→                "description": (r.get("description") or "")[:120],
    40→                "url": r["html_url"],
    41→                "updated": r["updated_at"][:10],
    42→                "language": r.get("language") or "—",
    43→            }
    44→            for r in data.get("items", [])[:max_results]
    45→        ]
    46→    except Exception as e:
    47→        print(f"GitHub search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    48→        return []
    49→

     1→"""Hacker News search source via Algolia API."""
     2→
     3→from __future__ import annotations
     4→
     5→import sys
     6→
     7→import httpx
     8→
     9→HN_API = "https://hn.algolia.com/api/v1"
    10→
    11→
    12→def search_discussions(
    13→    query: str,
    14→    max_results: int = 5,
    15→) -> list[dict]:
    16→    """Search Hacker News for discussions matching the query."""
    17→    url = f"{HN_API}/search"
    18→    params = {
    19→        "query": query,
    20→        "tags": "story",
    21→        "hitsPerPage": max_results,
    22→        "numericFilters": "points>5",
    23→    }
    24→    try:
    25→        resp = httpx.get(url, params=params, timeout=15)
    26→        resp.raise_for_status()
    27→        data = resp.json()
    28→        return [
    29→            {
    30→                "title": h["title"],
    31→                "points": h.get("points", 0),
    32→                "comments": h.get("num_comments", 0),
    33→                "url": f"https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id={h['objectID']}",
    34→                "date": h.get("created_at", "")[:10],
    35→            }
    36→            for h in data.get("hits", [])[:max_results]
    37→        ]
    38→    except Exception as e:
    39→        print(f"HN search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
    40→        return []
    41→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #36
Write TOOL CALL 
{
  "file_path": "/home/gem/project/src/priorart/scoring.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Reality signal computation from search results.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom datetime import date, datetime, timedelta\n\n_FUNDING_KEYWORDS = frozenset([\n    \"ycombinator\",\n    \"y combinator\",\n    \"yc w\",\n    \"yc s\",\n    \"backed by\",\n    \"funded by\",\n    \"raised\",\n    \"series a\",\n    \"series b\",\n    \"series c\",\n    \"sequoia\",\n    \"a16z\",\n    \"andreessen\",\n    \"venture\",\n    \"acquired\",\n])\n\n\ndef _parse_date(date_str: str) -> date | None:\n    \"\"\"Parse a YYYY-MM-DD date string, returning None on failure.\"\"\"\n    try:\n        return datetime.strptime(date_str[:10], \"%Y-%m-%d\").date()\n    except (ValueError, TypeError):\n        return None\n\n\ndef _recency_score(repos: list[dict], hn_posts: list[dict], today: date) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Compute recency score (0-10): recent activity scores higher.\n\n    Measures what fraction of items were updated within the last 365 days.\n    >= 50% recent \u2192 10, >= 25% recent \u2192 5, otherwise \u2192 0.\n    \"\"\"\n    dates: list[date] = []\n    for r in repos:\n        d = _parse_date(r.get(\"updated\", \"\"))\n        if d:\n            dates.append(d)\n    for h in hn_posts:\n        d = _parse_date(h.get(\"date\", \"\"))\n        if d:\n            dates.append(d)\n\n    if not dates:\n        return 0\n\n    cutoff = today - timedelta(days=365)\n    recent_count = sum(1 for d in dates if d >= cutoff)\n    fraction = recent_count / len(dates)\n\n    if fraction >= 0.5:\n        return 10\n    if fraction >= 0.25:\n        return 5\n    return 0\n\n\ndef _funding_score(repos: list[dict]) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Compute funding signal score (0-5) from GitHub repo descriptions.\n\n    Returns 5 if any repo description contains a known funding keyword.\n    \"\"\"\n    for r in repos:\n        desc = (r.get(\"description\") or \"\").lower()\n        if any(kw in desc for kw in _FUNDING_KEYWORDS):\n            return 5\n    return 0\n\n\ndef _velocity_score(repos: list[dict], hn_posts: list[dict], today: date) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Compute community velocity score (0-5): growing community scores higher.\n\n    Compares items updated in the last 6 months (recent) to items updated\n    6\u201324 months ago (older).\n    growing (recent >= older) \u2192 5, partial activity \u2192 2, stagnant \u2192 0.\n    \"\"\"\n    cutoff_recent = today - timedelta(days=180)\n    cutoff_older = today - timedelta(days=730)\n\n    recent = 0\n    older = 0\n\n    all_dates = [_parse_date(r.get(\"updated\", \"\")) for r in repos] + [\n        _parse_date(h.get(\"date\", \"\")) for h in hn_posts\n    ]\n\n    for d in all_dates:\n        if d is None:\n            continue\n        if d >= cutoff_recent:\n            recent += 1\n        elif d >= cutoff_older:\n            older += 1\n\n    if recent == 0 and older == 0:\n        return 0\n    if recent >= older:\n        return 5\n    if recent > 0:\n        return 2\n    return 0\n\n\ndef compute_signal(\n    repos: list[dict],\n    hn_posts: list[dict],\n    top_similarity: float | None = None,\n    today: date | None = None,\n) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Compute a 0-100 reality signal from search results.\n\n    Args:\n        repos: GitHub repository results.\n        hn_posts: Hacker News post results.\n        top_similarity: Optional average cosine similarity of the top results\n            to the query embedding (0\u20131). When provided, a semantic boost\n            component is added to the breakdown and score.\n        today: Reference date for recency/velocity calculations. Defaults to\n            today's date. Pass a fixed date in tests for determinism.\n\n    Returns:\n        Dict with ``score``, ``verdict``, and ``breakdown``.\n        Breakdown always includes: github, hn, recency, funding, velocity.\n        Breakdown includes ``semantic`` only when top_similarity is provided.\n    \"\"\"\n    if today is None:\n        today = date.today()\n\n    # GitHub component (0-40): repo count \u00d7 star quality\n    total_repos = len(repos)\n    max_stars = max((r[\"stars\"] for r in repos), default=0)\n\n    if total_repos == 0:\n        gh_score = 0\n    elif total_repos <= 3:\n        gh_score = 10\n    elif total_repos <= 7:\n        gh_score = 20\n    else:\n        gh_score = 30\n\n    if max_stars >= 5000:\n        gh_score = min(40, gh_score + 10)\n    elif max_stars >= 1000:\n        gh_score = min(40, gh_score + 8)\n    elif max_stars >= 100:\n        gh_score = min(40, gh_score + 5)\n\n    # HN component (0-25): post count \u00d7 point quality\n    total_hn = len(hn_posts)\n    max_points = max((p[\"points\"] for p in hn_posts), default=0)\n\n    if total_hn == 0:\n        hn_score = 0\n    elif total_hn <= 2:\n        hn_score = 7\n    else:\n        hn_score = 15\n\n    if max_points >= 100:\n        hn_score = min(25, hn_score + 10)\n    elif max_points >= 30:\n        hn_score = min(25, hn_score + 6)\n\n    # Semantic component (0-15): rewards conceptually similar results\n    semantic_score = 0\n    if top_similarity is not None:\n        if top_similarity >= 0.8:\n            semantic_score = 15\n        elif top_similarity >= 0.6:\n            semantic_score = 10\n        elif top_similarity >= 0.4:\n            semantic_score = 7\n        elif top_similarity >= 0.2:\n            semantic_score = 3\n\n    # Recency component (0-10): recent activity scores higher\n    recency_score = _recency_score(repos, hn_posts, today)\n\n    # Funding component (0-5): commercial backing signals\n    funding_score = _funding_score(repos)\n\n    # Velocity component (0-5): growing community scores higher\n    velocity_score = _velocity_score(repos, hn_posts, today)\n\n    score = min(\n        100,\n        gh_score + hn_score + semantic_score + recency_score + funding_score + velocity_score,\n    )\n\n    if score < 30:\n        verdict = \"LOW\"\n    elif score <= 60:\n        verdict = \"MODERATE\"\n    else:\n        verdict = \"HIGH\"\n\n    breakdown: dict[str, int] = {\n        \"github\": gh_score,\n        \"hn\": hn_score,\n        \"recency\": recency_score,\n        \"funding\": funding_score,\n        \"velocity\": velocity_score,\n    }\n    if top_similarity is not None:\n        breakdown[\"semantic\"] = semantic_score\n\n    return {\n        \"score\": score,\n        \"verdict\": verdict,\n        \"breakdown\": breakdown,\n    }\n"

compute_signal(repos, [], today=TODAY)\n        assert result[\"breakdown\"][\"recency\"] == 10\n        assert result[\"score\"] == 40  # gh=30 + recency=10\n\n\n#       make_repo(10, updated=VELOCITY_OLDER)\n        ]\n        result = compute_signal(repos, [], today=TODAY)\n        assert result[\"breakdown\"][\"velocity\"] == 5\n\n    def make_repo(10, updated=VELOCITY_OLDER),\n        ]\n        result = compute_signal(repos, [], today=TODAY)\n        assert result[\"breakdown\"][\"velocity\"] == 5\n\n    def test_declining_community_partial_velocity(self):\n        # More older (180\u2013730 days) than recent, but some recent \u2192 2\n        repos = [make_repo(10, updated=VELOCITY_RECENT)] + [\n            make_repo(10, updated=VELOCITY_OLDER)\n        ] * 3\n        result = compute_signal(repos, [], today=TODAY)\n        assert result[\"breakdown\"][\"velocity\"] == 2\n\n    def test_no_recent_only_older_zero_velocity(self):\n        # Items exist only in 180\u2013730 day window, none in last 180 \u2192 0\n        repos = [make_repo(10, updated=VELOCITY_OLDER)] * 3\n ASSISTANTMESSAGE #92
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/priorart/scoring.py` — Added `_recency_score`, `_funding_score`, `_velocity_score` helpers; updated `compute_signal` with three new components (recency 0-10, funding 0-5, velocity 0-5), adjusted GitHub (0-40), HN (0-25), semantic (0-15) caps; added injectable `today` param for test determinism - `src/priorart/formatters.py` — Added `_format_breakdown` helper; both `format_markdown` and `format_table` now render a "Signal Breakdown" line showing all per-source scores - `tests/test_scoring.py` — Rewrote all tier/verdict tests with updated expected values; added `TestRecencyComponent` (8 tests), `TestFundingComponent` (9 tests), `TestVelocityComponent` (8 tests), `TestCombinedSignal` (2 integration tests); 209 tests total, all passing - `tests/test_formatters.py` — Updated fixtures to include new breakdown keys; added breakdown display tests for markdown and table formatters ## Key Decisions - Rescaled existing component caps (GitHub 60→40, HN 40→25, Semantic 20→15) to make room for three new signals while keeping total cap at 100 - New `today: date | None` parameter defaults to `date.today()` in production but accepts a fixed date in tests for determinism - Recency threshold: ≥50% of items updated within 365 days → 10 pts; ≥25% → 5 pts - Velocity distinguishes "within 180 days" (growing) vs "180–730 days" (older); stale items (>730 days) are excluded from both windows - Funding detection is keyword-based on GitHub repo descriptions only (no HN), capped at a flat 5 pts regardless of how many repos match ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-199-enhanced-signal-scoring` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/priorart/pull/3
